General guidelines.
   - When you execute commands, always save their logs to files for easier reading if the output becomes large.
   - When running commands, do not set a timeout yourself — let them run as long as needed (default timeout - 2 minutes is more than enough), and once they finish, review the logs in the file.

      This detailed investigation is especially helpful when user mentions CI failures, asks to investigate logs, you see non-passing status, or when finalizing a PR.
      Note: If user says \"failing\" but tools show \"passing\", this might indicate stale data - consider downloading fresh logs and checking timestamps to resolve the discrepancy.
   - When a code or log file has more than 1500 lines, read it in chunks of 1500 lines.
   - When facing a complex problem, do as much tracing as possible and turn on all verbose modes.

This is **not** for general desktop use - it's for isolated environments where you want maximum AI agent freedom.\n    67→\n    68→**OpenCode Compatibility**: We maintain 100% compatibility with OpenCode's JSON event streaming format, so tools expecting `opencode run --format json --model opencode/grok-code` output will work with our agent-cli.\n    69→\n    70→## Features\n    71→\n    72→- **JSON Input/Output**: Accepts JSON via stdin, outputs JSON event streams (OpenCode-compatible)\n    73→- **Plain Text Input**: Also accepts plain text messages (auto-converted to JSON format)\n    74→- **Unrestricted Access**: Full file system and command execution access (no sandbox, no restrictions)\n    75→- **Tool Support**: 13 tools including websearch, codesearch, batch - all enabled by default\n    76→- **Flexible Model Selection**: Supports [OpenCode Zen](https://opencode.ai/docs/zen/), [Claude OAuth](docs/claude-oauth.md), [Groq](docs/groq.md), [OpenRouter](docs/openrouter.md), and more - see [MODELS.md](MODELS.md)\n    77→- **Public Domain**: Unlicense - use it however you want\n    78→\n    79→## Quick Start\n    80→\n    81→**Plain text (easiest):**\n    82→\n    83→```bash\n    84→echo \"hi\" | agent\n    85→```\n    86→\n    87→**Simple JSON message:**\n    88→\n    89→```bash\n    90→echo '{\"message\":\"hi\"}' | agent\n    91→```\n    92→\n    93→**With custom model:**\n    94→\n    95→```bash\n    96→echo \"hi\" | agent --model opencode/grok-code\n    97→```\n    98→\n    99→**Direct prompt mode:**\n   100→\n   101→```bash\n   102→agent -p \"What is 2+2?\"\n   103→```\n   104→\n   105→See [js/README.md](js/README.md#usage) for more usage examples including model selection, session resume, and JSON output standards.\n   106→\n   107→## Supported Tools\n   108→\n   109→All 13 tools are **enabled by default** with **no configuration required**. See [TOOLS.md](TOOLS.md) for complete documentation.\n   110→\n   111→### File Operations\n   112→\n   113→- **`read`** - Read file contents\n   114→- **`write`** - Write files\n   115→- **`edit`** - Edit files with string replacement\n   116→- **`list`** - List directory contents\n   117→\n   118→### Search Tools\n   119→\n   120→- **`glob`** - File pattern matching (`**/*.js`)\n   121→- **`grep`** - Text search with regex support\n   122→- **`websearch`** ✨ - Web search via Exa API (no config needed!)\n   123→- **`codesearch`** ✨ - Code search via Exa API (no config needed!)\n   124→\n   125→### Execution Tools\n   126→\n   127→- **`bash`** - Execute shell commands\n   128→- **`batch`** ✨ - Batch multiple tool calls (no config needed!)\n   129→- **`task`** - Launch subagent tasks\n   130→\n   131→### Utility Tools\n   132→\n   133→- **`todo`** - Task tracking\n   134→- **`webfetch`** - Fetch and process URLs\n   135→\n   136→✨ = Always enabled (no experimental flags or environment variables needed)\n   137→\n   138→## Architecture\n   139→\n   140→This agent reproduces OpenCode's `run --format json` command architecture:\n   141→\n   142→- **Streaming JSON Events**: Real-time event stream output\n   143→- **Event Types**: `tool_use`, `text`, `step_start`, `step_finish`, `error`\n   144→- **Session Management**: Unique session IDs for each request\n   145→- **Tool Execution**: Tools with unrestricted access\n   146→- **Compatible Format**: Events match OpenCode's JSON schema exactly\n   147→\n   148→## MCP (Model Context Protocol) Support\n   149→\n   150→The agent supports the Model Context Protocol (MCP), allowing you to extend functionality with MCP servers such as browser automation via Playwright.\n   151→\n   152→**Quick setup for Playwright MCP:**\n   153→\n   154→```bash\n   155→agent mcp add playwright npx @playwright/mcp@latest\n   156→```\n   157→\n   158→See [js/README.md](js/README.md#mcp-model-context-protocol-support) for full MCP We reproduce OpenCode's `run --format json --model opencode/grok-code` mode with:\n    24→\n    25→- ✅ **JSON Input/Output**: Compatible with `opencode run --format json --model opencode/grok-code`\n    26→- ✅ **Plain Text Input**: Also accepts plain text messages (auto-converted to JSON format)\n    27→- ✅ **Flexible Model Selection**: Defaults to free OpenCode Zen Grok Code Fast 1, supports [OpenCode Zen](https://opencode.ai/docs/zen/), [Claude OAuth](../docs/claude-oauth.md), [Groq](../docs/groq.md), and [OpenRouter](../docs/openrouter.md) providers\n    28→- ✅ **No Restrictions**: Fully unrestricted file system and command execution access (no sandbox)\n    29→- ✅ **Minimal Footprint**: Built with Bun.sh for maximum efficiency\n    30→- ✅ **Full Tool Support**: 13 tools including websearch, codesearch, batch - all enabled by default\n    31→- ✅ **100% OpenCode Compatible**: All tool outputs match OpenCode's JSON format exactly\n    32→- ✅ **Internal HTTP Server**: Uses local HTTP server for session management (not exposed externally)\n    33→- ❌ **No TUI**: Pure JSON CLI interface only\n    34→- ❌ **No Sandbox**: Designed for VMs/containers where full access is acceptable\n    35→- ❌ **No LSP**: No Language Server Protocol support for diagnostics\n    36→- ❌ **No Permissions**: No permission system - Check and remove lines referencing `~/.bun/bin` from:\n    87→\n    88→- `~/.bashrc`\n    89→- `~/.zshrc`\n    90→- `~/.config/fish/config.fish`\n    91→\n    92→Or the corresponding configuration file for your shell.\n    93→\n    94→## Usage\n    95→\n    96→### Simplest Examples\n    97→\n    98→**Plain text (easiest):**\n    99→\n   100→```bash\n   101→echo \"hi\" | agent\n   102→```\n   103→\n   104→**Simple JSON message:**\n   105→\n   106→```bash\n   107→echo '{\"message\":\"hi\"}' | agent\n   108→```\n   109→\n   110→**With custom model:**\n   111→\n   112→```bash\n   113→echo \"hi\" | agent --model opencode/grok-code\n   114→```\n   115→\n   116→### More Examples\n   117→\n   118→**Plain Text Input:**\n   119→\n   120→```bash\n   121→echo \"hello world\" | agent\n   122→echo \"search the web for TypeScript news\" | agent\n   123→```\n   124→\n   125→**JSON Input with tool calls:**\n   126→\n   127→```bash\n   128→echo '{\"message\":\"run command\",\"tools\":[{\"name\":\"bash\",\"params\":{\"command\":\"ls -la\"}}]}' | agent\n   129→```\n   130→\n   131→**Using different models:**\n   132→\n   133→```bash\n   134→# Default model (free Grok Code Fast 1)\n   135→echo \"hi\" | agent\n   136→\n   137→# Other free models\n   138→echo \"hi\" | agent --model opencode/big-pickle\n   139→echo \"hi\" | agent --model opencode/gpt-5-nano\n   140→\n   141→# Premium models (OpenCode Zen subscription)\n   142→echo \"hi\" | agent --model opencode/sonnet        # Claude Sonnet 4.5\n   143→echo \"hi\" | agent --model opencode/haiku         # Claude Haiku 4.5\n   144→echo \"hi\" | agent --model opencode/opus          # Claude Opus 4.1\n   145→echo \"hi\" | agent --model opencode/gemini-3-pro  # Gemini 3 Pro\n   146→\n   147→# Groq models (requires GROQ_API_KEY)\n   148→echo \"hi\" | agent --model groq/llama-3.3-70b-versatile  # Llama 3.3 70B\n   149→echo \"hi\" | agent --model groq/llama-3.1-8b-instant     # Llama 3.1 8B (fast)\n   150→\n   151→# OpenRouter models (requires OPENROUTER_API_KEY)\n   152→echo \"hi\" | agent --model openrouter/anthropic/claude-sonnet-4  # Claude via OpenRouter\n   153→echo \"hi\" | agent --model openrouter/openai/gpt-4o              # GPT-4o via OpenRouter\n   154→echo \"hi\" | agent --model openrouter/meta-llama/llama-3.3-70b   # Llama via OpenRouter\n   155→\n   156→# Anthropic direct (requires ANTHROPIC_API_KEY)\n   157→echo \"hi\" | agent --model anthropic/claude-sonnet-4-5  # Claude Sonnet 4.5\n   158→echo \"hi\" | agent --model anthropic/claude-opus-4-1    # Claude Opus 4.1\n   159→\n   160→# Anthropic OAuth (requires Claude Pro/Max subscription)\n   161→agent auth login                                       # Select Anthropic > Claude Pro/Max\n   162→echo \"hi\" | agent --model anthropic/claude-sonnet-4-5  # Uses OAuth credentials\n   163→\n   164→# Use existing Claude Code CLI credentials\n   165→echo \"hi\" | agent --use-existing-claude-oauth          # Reads from ~/.claude/.credentials.json\n   166→\n   167→# Google Gemini (requires GOOGLE_API_KEY)\n   168→echo \"hi\" | agent --model google/gemini-3-pro          # Gemini 3 Pro\n   169→echo \"hi\" | agent --model google/gemini-2.5-flash      # Gemini 2.5 Flash\n   170→\n   171→# GitHub Copilot (requires Copilot subscription)\n   172→agent auth login                                       # Select GitHub Copilot\n   173→echo \"hi\" | agent --model github-copilot/gpt-4o        # Uses Copilot\n   174→```\n   175→\n   176→See [MODELS.md](../MODELS.md) for complete list of available models and pricing.\n   177→See [docs/groq.md](../docs/groq.md) for Groq provider documentation.\n   178→See [docs/openrouter.md](../docs/openrouter.md) for OpenRouter provider documentation.\n   179→See [docs/claude-oauth.md](../docs/claude-oauth.md) for Claude OAuth provider documentation.\n   180→\n   181→### Direct Prompt Mode\n   182→\n   183→Use `-p`/`--prompt` to send a prompt directly without reading from stdin:\n   184→\n   185→```bash\n   186→# Direct prompt (bypasses stdin)\n   187→agent -p \"What is 2+2?\"\n   188→\n   189→# Useful in scripts\n   190→result=$(agent -p \"Summarize: $(cat file.txt)\")\n   191→```\n   192→\n   193→### Session Resume\n   194→\n   195→Resume or continue previous sessions:\n   196→\n   197→```bash\n   198→# Continue the most recent session (creates a fork with new UUID by default)\n   199→echo \"Continue where we left off\" | agent --continue\n   200→\n   201→# Short form\n   202→echo \"Continue where we left off\" | agent -c\n   203→\n   204→# Resume a specific session by ID (creates a fork with new UUID by default)\n   205→echo \"Let's continue\" | agent --resume ses_abc123xyz\n   206→\n   207→# Continue in the same session without forking\n   208→echo \"Keep going\" | agent --continue --no-fork\n   209→\n   210→# Resume specific session without forking\n   211→echo \"Keep going\" | agent --resume ses_abc123xyz --no-fork\n   212→```\n   213→\n   214→**Note**: By default, `--resume` and `--continue` create a new session ID (fork) to preserve the original conversation history. Use `--no-fork` to continue in the same session.\n   215→\n   216→## CLI Options\n   217→\n   218→```bash\n   219→agent [options]\n   220→\n   221→Options:\n   222→  --model                        Model to use in format providerID/modelID\n   223→                                 Default: opencode/grok-code\n   224→  --json-standard                JSON output format standard\n   225→                                 Choices: \"opencode\" (default), \"claude\" (experimental)\n   226→  --use-existing-claude-oauth    Use existing Claude OAuth credentials\n   227→                                 from ~/.claude/.credentials.json\n   228→  --system-message               Full override of the system message\n   229→  --system-message-file          Full override of the system message from file\n   230→  --append-system-message        Append to the default system message\n   231→  --append-system-message-file   Append to the default system message from file\n   232→\n   233→Stdin Mode Options:\n   234→  -p, --prompt                   Direct prompt (bypasses stdin reading)\n   235→  --disable-stdin                Disable stdin streaming (requires --prompt)\n   236→  --stdin-stream-timeout         Timeout in ms for stdin reading (default: none)\n   237→  --interactive                  Accept plain text input (default: true)\n   238→  --no-interactive               Only accept JSON input\n   239→  --auto-merge-queued-messages   Merge rapidly arriving lines (default: true)\n   240→  --no-auto-merge-queued-messages Treat each line as separate message\n   241→  --always-accept-stdin          Keep accepting input after agent finishes (default: true)\n   242→  --no-always-accept-stdin       Single-message mode - exit after first response\n   243→  --compact-json                 Output compact JSON for program-to-program use\n   244→\n   245→Session Resume Options:\n   246→  -r, --resume <sessionID>       Resume a specific session by ID\n   247→                                 By default, forks with a new UUID\n   248→  -c, --continue                 Continue the most recent session\n   249→                                 By default, forks with a new UUID\n   250→  --no-fork                      When used with --resume or --continue,\n   251→                                 continue in the same session without forking\n   252→\n   253→  --help                         Show help\n   254→  --version                      Show version number\n   255→\n   256→Commands:\n   257→  auth login           Authenticate with a provider (Anthropic, GitHub Copilot, etc.)\n   258→  auth logout          Remove credentials for a provider\n   259→  auth list            List configured credentials\n   260→  auth status          Check authentication status (experimental)\n   261→  mcp                  MCP server commands\n   262→```\n   263→\n   264→See [docs/stdin-mode.md](../docs/stdin-mode.md) for comprehensive stdin mode documentation.\n   265→\n   266→### JSON Output Standards\n   267→\n   268→The agent supports two JSON output format standards via the `--json-standard` option:\n   269→\n   270→#### OpenCode Standard (default)\n   271→\n   272→The OpenCode format is the default JSON output format, compatible with `opencode run --format json`:\n   273→\n   274→```bash\n   275→echo \"hi\" | agent --json-standard opencode\n   276→```\n   277→\n   278→- **Format**: Pretty-printed JSON (human-readable with indentation)\n   279→- **Event Types**: `step_start`, `step_finish`, `text`, `tool_use`, `error`\n   280→- **Timestamps**: Unix milliseconds (number)\n   281→- **Session ID**: `sessionID` (camelCase)\n   282→\n   283→#### Claude Standard (experimental)\n   284→\n   285→The Claude format provides compatibility with Anthropic's Claude CLI `--output-format stream-json`:\n   286→\n   287→```bash\n   288→echo \"hi\" | agent --json-standard claude\n   289→```\n   290→\n   291→- **Format**: NDJSON (Newline-Delimited JSON - compact, one JSON per line)\n   292→- **Event Types**: `init`, `message`, `tool_use`, `tool_result`, `result`\n   293→- **Timestamps**: ISO 8601 strings\n   294→- **Session ID**: `session_id` (snake_case)\n   295→\n   296→### Input Formats\n   297→\n   298→**Plain Text (auto-converted):**\n   299→\n   300→```bash\n   301→echo \"your message here\" | agent\n   302→```\n   303→\n   304→**JSON Format:**\n   305→\n   306→```json\n   307→{\n   308→  \"message\": \"Your message here\",\n   309→  \"tools\": [\n   310→    {\n   311→      \"name\": \"bash\",\n   312→      \"params\": { \"command\": \"ls -la\" }\n   313→    }\n   314→  ]\n   315→}\n   316→```\n   317→\n   318→## Supported Tools\n   319→\n   320→All 13 tools are **enabled by default** with **no configuration required**. See [TOOLS.md](../TOOLS.md) for complete documentation.\n   321→\n   322→### File Operations\n   323→\n   324→- **`read`** - Read file contents\n   325→- **`write`** - Write files\n   326→- **`edit`** - Edit files with string replacement\n   327→- **`list`** - List directory contents\n   328→\n   329→### Search Tools\n   330→\n   331→- **`glob`** - File pattern matching (`**/*.js`)\n   332→- **`grep`** - Text search with regex support\n   333→- **`websearch`** ✨ - Web search via Exa API (no config needed!)\n   334→- **`codesearch`** ✨ - Code search via Exa API (no config needed!)\n   335→\n   336→### Execution Tools\n   337→\n   338→- **`bash`** - Execute shell commands\n   339→- **`batch`** ✨ - Batch multiple tool calls (no config needed!)\n   340→- **`task`** - Launch subagent tasks\n   341→\n   342→### Utility Tools\n   343→\n   344→- **`todo`** - Task tracking\n   345→- **`webfetch`** - Fetch and process URLs\n   346→\n   347→✨ = Always enabled (no experimental flags or environment variables needed)\n   348→\n   349→## MCP (Model Context Protocol) Support\n   350→\n   351→The agent supports the Model Context Protocol (MCP), allowing you to extend functionality with MCP servers. MCP enables the agent to interact with external tools and services, such as browser automation via Playwright.\n   352→\n   353→### Installing Playwright MCP\n   354→\n   355→Microsoft's Playwright MCP server provides browser automation capabilities using Playwright. This enables the agent to interact with web pages through structured accessibility snapshots.\n   356→\n   357→**Requirements:**\n   358→\n   359→- Node.js 18 or newer (for running the Playwright MCP server)\n   360→- Bun (for running the agent itself)\n   361→\n   362→**Installation:**\n   363→\n   364→```bash\n   365→# Add Playwright MCP server to your agent configuration\n   366→agent mcp add playwright npx @playwright/mcp@latest\n   367→\n   368→# Verify the configuration\n   369→agent mcp list\n   370→```\n   371→\n   372→This will create a configuration file at `~/.config/link-assistant-agent/opencode.json` (or your system's config directory) with:\n   373→\n   374→```json\n   375→{\n   376→  \"$schema\": \"https://opencode.ai/config.json\",\n   377→  \"mcp\": {\n   378→    \"playwright\": {\n   379→      \"type\": \"local\",\n   380→      \"command\": [\"npx\", \"@playwright/mcp@latest\"],\n   381→      \"enabled\": true\n   382→    }\n   383→  }\n   384→}\n   385→```\n   386→\n   387→**Available Playwright Tools:**\n   388→\n   389→Once configured, the agent gains access to 22+ browser automation tools:\n   390→\n   391→- `browser_navigate` - Navigate to a URL\n   392→- `browser_click` - Click on an element\n   393→- `browser_type` - Type text into an element\n   394→- `browser_snapshot` - Capture accessibility snapshot\n   395→- `browser_take_screenshot` - Take a screenshot\n   396→- `browser_fill_form` - Fill multiple form fields\n   397→- `browser_select_option` - Select dropdown option\n   398→- `browser_hover` - Hover over element\n   399→- `browser_drag` - Drag and drop\n   400→- `browser_evaluate` - Execute JavaScript\n   401→- `browser_tabs` - Manage browser tabs\n   402→- `browser_close` - Close the browser\n   403→- `browser_wait_for` - Wait for text/element\n   404→- `browser_press_key` - Press keyboard key\n   405→- `browser_handle_dialog` - Handle browser dialogs\n   406→- `browser_network_requests` - Get network requests\n   407→- `browser_console_messages` - Get console messages\n   408→- `browser_file_upload` - Upload files\n   409→- `browser_resize` - Resize browser window\n   410→- `browser_navigate_back` - Navigate back\n   411→- `browser_install` - Install browser\n   412→- `browser_run_code` - Run Playwright code\n   413→\n   414→**Usage Example:**\n   415→\n   416→```bash\n   417→# Tell the agent to navigate to a website and take a screenshot\n   418→echo \"Navigate to https://example.com and take a screenshot\" | agent\n   419→```\n   420→\n   421→The agent will automatically use the Playwright MCP tools when browser automation is needed.\n   422→\n   423→**Learn More:**\n   424→\n   425→- [Playwright MCP GitHub Repository](https://github.com/microsoft/playwright-mcp)\n   426→- [Using Playwright MCP with Claude Code](https://til.simonwillison.net/claude-code/playwright-mcp-claude-code)\n   427→- [Playwright MCP Case Study](../docs/case-studies/playwright-mcp-support/case-study.md)\n   428→\n   429→### Managing MCP Servers\n   430→\n   431→**List configured servers:**\n   432→\n   433→```bash\n   434→agent mcp list\n   435→```\n   436→\n   437→**Add a remote MCP server:**\n   438→\n   439→```bash\n   440→agent mcp add myserver --url https://example.com/mcp\n   441→```\n   442→\n   443→**Interactive mode:**\n   444→\n   445→If you prefer an interactive setup, just run:\n   446→\n   447→```bash\n   448→agent mcp add\n   449→```\n   450→\n   451→The interactive prompt will guide you through configuring local or remote MCP servers.\n   452→\n   453→## Key Features\n   454→\n   455→### No Configuration Required\n   456→\n   457→- **WebSearch/CodeSearch**: Work without `LINK_ASSISTANT_AGENT_EXPERIMENTAL_EXA` environment variable (legacy `OPENCODE_EXPERIMENTAL_EXA` still supported)\n   458→- **Batch Tool**: Always enabled, no experimental flag needed\n   459→- **All Tools**: No config files, API keys handled automatically\n   460→\n   461→### OpenCode 100% Compatible\n   462→\n   463→- All tools produce JSON output matching OpenCode's exact format\n   464→- WebSearch and CodeSearch tools are verified 100% compatible\n   465→- Tool event structure matches OpenCode specifications\n   466→- Can be used as drop-in replacement for `opencode run --format json`\n   467→\n   468→### Plain Text Support\n   469→\n   470→Both plain text and JSON input work:\n   471→\n   472→```bash\n   473→# Plain text\n   474→echo \"hello\" | bun run src/index.js\n   475→\n   476→# JSON\n   477→echo '{\"message\":\"hello\"}' | bun run src/index.js\n   478→```\n   479→\n   480→Plain text is automatically converted to `{\"message\":\"your text\"}` format.\n   481→\n   482→### JSON Event Streaming Output\n   483→\n   484→JSON output is pretty-printed for easy readability while maintaining OpenCode compatibility:\n   485→\n   486→```bash\n   487→echo \"hi\" | agent\n   488→```\n   489→\n   490→Output (pretty-printed JSON events):\n   491→\n   492→```json\n   493→{\n   494→  \"type\": \"step_start\",\n   495→  \"timestamp\": 1763618628840,\n   496→ Create a changeset:\n   585→\n   586→   ```bash\n   587→   bun run changeset\n   588→   ```\n   589→\n   590→2. Version the package:\n   591→\n   592→   ```bash\n   593→   bun run changeset:version\n   594→   ```\n   595→\n   596→3. Publish to npm:\n   597→   ```bash\n   598→   bun run changeset:publish\n   599→   ```\n   600→\n   601→The package publishes source files directly (no build step required). Bun handles TypeScript execution natively.\n   602→\n   603→## Why Bun-only? No Node.js or Deno support?\n   604→\n   605→This agent is **exclusively built for Bun** for the following reasons:\n   606→\n   607→1. **Faster Development**: No compilation step - direct execution with `bun run`\n   608→2. **Simpler Dependencies**: Fewer dev dependencies, no TypeScript compiler overhead\n   609→3. **Performance**: Bun's fast runtime and native ESM support\n   610→4. **Minimalism**: Single runtime target keeps the codebase simple\n   611→5. **Bun Ecosystem**: Leverages Bun-specific features and optimizations\n   612→\n   613→**Not supporting Node.js or Deno is intentional** to keep the project focused and minimal. If you need Node.js/Deno compatibility, consider using [OpenCode](https://github.com/sst/opencode) instead.\n   614→\n   615→## Project Structure\n   616→\n   617→```\n   618→js/\n   619→├── src/           # Source code\n   620→│   ├── index.js   # Main entry point with JSON/plain text input support\n   621→│   ├── session/   # Session management and agent implementation\n   622→│   └── tool/      # Tool implementations\n   623→├── tests/         # Comprehensive test suite\n   624→├── experiments/   # Experimental code\n   625→├── package.json   # npm package configuration\n   626→└── tsconfig.json  # TypeScript configuration\n   627→```\n   628→\n   629→## Architecture\n   630→\n   631→This agent-cli reproduces the core architecture of [OpenCode](https://github.com/sst/opencode)'s `run --format json` command:\n   632→\n   633→- **Streaming JSON Events**: Instead of single responses, outputs real-time event stream\n   634→- **Event Types**: `tool_use`, `text`, `step_start`, `step_finish`, `error`\n   635→- **Session Management**: Each request gets a unique session ID\n   636→- **Tool Execution**: 13 tools with unrestricted access (bash, read, write, edit, list, glob, grep, websearch, codesearch, batch, task, todo, webfetch)\n   637→- **Compatible Format**: Events match OpenCode's JSON schema for interoperability\n   638→\n   639→The agent streams events as they occur, providing the same real-time experience as OpenCode's JSON mode.\n   640→\n   641→## Examples\n   642→\n   643→See [EXAMPLES.md](../EXAMPLES.md) for detailed usage examples of each tool with both agent-cli and opencode commands.\n   644→\n   645→## Documentation\n   646→\n   647→For full documentation, see the [main README](../README.md) in the repository root.\n   648→\n   649→- [Models and Pricing](../MODELS.md)\n   650→- [Tools Reference](../TOOLS.md)\n   651→- [Usage Examples](../EXAMPLES.md)\n   652→- [Testing Guide](../TESTING.md)\n   653→\n   654→## License\n   655→\n   656→Unlicense (Public Domain)\n   657→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. // Log version and command info in verbose mode using lazy logging\n   235→  Log.Default.info(() => ({\n   236→    message: 'Agent started',\n   237→    version: pkg.version,\n   238→    command: 376→  systemMessage,\n   377→  appendSystemMessage,\n   378→  jsonStandard\n   379→) {\n   380→  const compactJson = argv['compact-json'] === true;\n   381→\n   382→  // Start server like OpenCode 394→      sessionID = resumeInfo.sessionID;\n   395→    } else {\n   396→      // Create a new session\n   397→      const createRes = await fetch(\n   398→ 418→      createBusEventSubscription({\n   419→        sessionID,\n   420→        eventHandler,\n   421→        onError: () => {\n   422→          hasError = true;\n   423→        },\n   424→ 456→\n   457→    // Wait for session to become idle\n   458→    await eventPromise;\n   459→  } finally {\n   460→    // Always clean up resources\n   461→    if (unsub) {\n   462→      unsub();\n   463→    }\n   464→    server.stop();\n   465→    await Instance.dispose();\n   466→  }\n   467→}\n   468→\n   469→async function runDirectMode(\n   470→  argv,\n   471→  request,\n   472→         eventHandler.output({\n   337→            type: 'text',\n   338→            timestamp: Date.now(),\n   339→            sessionID,\n   340→            part,\n   341→          });\n   342→ 408→  } finally {\n   409→    if (stdinReader) {\n   410→      stdinReader.stop();\n   411→    }\n   412→    if (unsub) {\n   413→      unsub();\n   414→    }\n   415→    server.stop();\n   416→    await Instance.dispose();\n   417→  }\n   418→}\n   419→\n   420→/**\n   421→ * Run direct mode with continuous stdin input\n   422→ * Keeps the session alive and processes messages as they arrive\n         "content": "     1→/**\n     2→ * Input queue for managing continuous stdin input.\n     3→ * Supports queuing of multiple messages and auto-merging of rapidly arriving lines.\n     4→ */\n     5→export class InputQueue {\n     6→  constructor(options = {}) {\n     7→    this.queue = [];\n     8→    this.autoMerge = options.autoMerge !== false; // enabled by default\n     9→    this.mergeDelayMs = options.mergeDelayMs || 50; // delay to wait for more lines\n    10→    this.pendingLines = [];\n    11→    this.mergeTimer = null;\n    12→    this.onMessage = options.onMessage || (() => {});\n    13→    this.interactive = options.interactive !== false; // enabled by default\n    14→  }\n    15→\n    16→  /**\n    17→   * Parse input and determine if it's JSON or plain text\n    18→   * @param {string} input - PROJECT STRUCTURE & TYPE\n\n**What is it?**\nLink Assistant Agent is a **minimal, public domain AI CLI agent** that provides OpenCode-compatible JSON interface for AI-powered task automation. It's designed for running in isolated environments (VMs, Docker) with unrestricted access.\n\n**Key Characteristics:**\n- **Public Domain** (Unlicense)\n- **Bun-only runtime** (requires Bun >= 1.0.0, NOT Node.js/Deno)\n- **Zero security restrictions** - full file system and command execution access\n- **100% OpenCode compatible** - can replace `opencode run --format json`\n- **Dual implementations**: JavaScript/Bun (production-ready) and Rust (WIP)\n\n### 2. MAIN SOURCE STRUCTURE\n\n```\njs/                          # JavaScript/Bun implementation (primary)\n├── src/\n│   ├── index.js            # Main entry point, CLI argument parsing\n│   ├── cli/\n│   │   ├── continuous-mode.js    # Entry point and CLI parsing\n│   ├── tool/                     # 7 implemented tools\n│   └── util/, error.rs           # Utilities\n└── Cargo.toml\n```\n\n### 3. HOW THE CLI/AGENT WORKS\n\n**Entry Point & Flow:**\n\n1. **Main Entry** (`js/src/index.js`)\n   - Parses CLI arguments with yargs\n   - Supports 3 modes: `--prompt`, continuous stdin (pipe), or interactive terminal\n   - Handles JSON/plain text input auto-conversion\n   - Sets up error handlers for uncaught exceptions/rejections\n\n2. **Input Handling**\n   - **Direct prompt mode**: `-p \"message\"` bypasses stdin\n   - **Piped stdin**: Reads from stdin, supports `--stdin-stream-timeout`\n   - **Interactive terminal**: Shows status messages, accepts manual input\n   - **Auto-merge**: Rapidly arriving lines are merged into single messages (50ms delay)\n\n3. **Processing Modes**\n\n   **Single-message mode** (default):\n   - `readStdinWithTimeout()` reads one message with optional timeout\n   - Calls `runAgentMode()` → processes single request → exits\n\n   **Continuous mode** (`--always-accept-stdin`):\n   - `runContinuousAgentMode()` keeps session alive\n   - `createContinuousStdinReader()` continuously reads from stdin\n   - Messages queued and processed sequentially\n   - Waits for `session.idle` event before processing next message\n\n4. **Server vs Direct Mode**\n   - **Server mode** (default): Spawns HTTP server, communicates via fetch()\n   - **Direct mode**: Single process, calls `SessionPrompt.prompt()` directly\n\n5. **Event Flow**\n   - `Bus.subscribeAll()` listens to session events: `message.part.updated`, `session.idle`, `session.error`\n   - Events transformed to JSON output: `step_start`, `text`, `tool_use`, `step_finish`, `error`\n   - Format controlled by `--json-standard` (opencode or claude)\n\n### 4. TIMEOUT-RELATED CODE\n\n**Key timeout locations:**\n\n1. **Stdin reading timeout** (`index.js`):\n   ```javascript\n   const timeout = argv['stdin-stream-timeout'] ?? null;  // ms\n   const input = await readStdinWithTimeout(timeout);\n   // Default: no timeout (wait indefinitely until EOF)\n   ```\n\n2. **Bash tool execution timeout** (`src/tool/bash.ts`):\n   ```javascript\n   const DEFAULT_TIMEOUT = 1 * 60 * 1000;    // 1 minute\n   const MAX_TIMEOUT = 10 * 60 * 1000;       // 10 minutes\n   const timeout = Math.min(params.timeout ?? DEFAULT_TIMEOUT, MAX_TIMEOUT);\n   \n   const timeoutTimer = setTimeout(() => {\n     timedOut = true;\n     void killTree();  // Kill process group\n   }, timeout);\n   ```\n\n3. **Continuous mode polling** (`continuous-mode.js`):\n   ```javascript\n   const checkRunning = setInterval(() => {\n     if (!stdinReader.isRunning()) {\n       // Wait for pending messages to complete\n       const waitForPending = () => {\n         if (!isProcessing && pendingMessages.length === 0) {\n           resolve();\n         } else {\n           setTimeout(waitForPending, 100);  // Polls every 100ms\n         }\n       };\n       waitForPending();\n     }\n   }, 100);\n   ```\n\n4. **Input queue merge delay** (`input-queue.js`):\n   ```javascript\n   this.mergeDelayMs = options.mergeDelayMs || 50;  // Wait 50ms for more lines\n   this.mergeTimer = setTimeout(() => {\n     this.flushPendingLines();\n   }, this.mergeDelayMs);\n   ```\n\n**Issue #146 Context:**\n- Process hung indefinitely after completing work\n- System message shows \"✅ Agent command completed\" at 15:37 but process didn't exit until manually killed ~2 hours later\n- Root cause: Some waitable resource (session.idle event?) not firing or not being properly awaited\n\n### 5. PROCESS EXECUTION & WAITING\n\n**Bash Tool** (`src/tool/bash.ts`):\n- Uses Node's `spawn()` with `stdio: ['ignore', 'pipe', 'pipe']`\n- Collects stdout/stderr output with event listeners\n- Implements timeout with `setTimeout()` + process group killing\n- For Unix: `process.kill(-pid, 'SIGTERM')` then `SIGKILL` after 200ms\n- For Windows: Uses `taskkill` command\n- Waits on promise: `proc.once('exit')` or `proc.once('error')`\n\n**Session Processing** (`session/prompt.ts`):\n- `SessionPrompt.prompt()` called to start message processing\n- Calls agent model via provider (OpenCode SDK or other LLM)\n- Emits events through Bus system\n\n**Event-driven Waiting**:\n- Client code waits on promises that resolve on `session.idle` event\n- In `continuous-mode.js`: \n  ```javascript\n  const messagePromise = new Promise((resolve) => {\n    const checkIdle = Bus.subscribeAll((event) => {\n      if (event.type === 'session.idle' && \n          event.properties.sessionID === sessionID) {\n        checkIdle();  // unsubscribe\n        resolve();\n      }\n    });\n  });\n  await messagePromise;  // Wait for session to finish\n  ```\n\n### 6. PACKAGE.json & DEPENDENCIES\n\n**Key Info**:\n- **Version**: 0.8.11\n- **Engine**: Requires Bun >= 1.0.0\n- **Type**: ES modules (`\"type\": \"module\"`)\n- **Bin**: `./src/index.js`\n\n**Notable Dependencies**:\n- `@opencode-ai/sdk` - OpenCode API client\n- `ai` - Vercel AI SDK (6.0.0-beta)\n- `@modelcontextprotocol/sdk` - MCP protocol support\n- `hono` - Web framework for server mode\n- `zod` - Schema validation\n- `yargs` - CLI argument parsing\n- `command-stream` - Command execution\n- `glob`, `minimatch` - File pattern matching\n- `tree-sitter-bash`, `web-tree-sitter` - Bash parsing\n- `@actions/github` - GitHub integration\n- `clipboardy` - Clipboard access\n\n**Dev Dependencies**:\n- ESLint, Prettier - Code formatting\n- Husky, lint-staged - Git hooks\n- Changesets - Release management\n\n### 7. HOW THE CLI/AGENT WORKS\n\n**Entry Point & Flow:**\n\n1. **Main Entry** (`js/src/index.js`)\n   - Parses CLI arguments with yargs\n   - Supports 3 modes: `--prompt`, continuous stdin (pipe), or interactive terminal\n   - Handles JSON/plain text input auto-conversion\n   - Sets up error handlers for uncaught exceptions/rejections\n\n2. **Input Handling**\n   - **Direct prompt mode**: `-p \"message\"` bypasses stdin\n   - **Piped stdin**: Reads from stdin, supports `--stdin-stream-timeout`\n   - **Interactive terminal**: Shows status messages, accepts manual input\n   - **Auto-merge**: Rapidly arriving lines are merged into single messages (50ms delay)\n\n3. **Processing Modes**\n\n   **Single-message mode** (default):\n   - `readStdinWithTimeout()` reads one message with optional timeout\n   - Calls `runAgentMode()` → processes single request → exits\n\n   **Continuous mode** (`--always-accept-stdin`):\n   - `runContinuousAgentMode()` keeps session alive\n   - `createContinuousStdinReader()` continuously reads from stdin\n   - Messages queued and processed sequentially\n   - Waits for `session.idle` event before processing next message\n\n4. **Server vs Direct Mode**\n   - **Server mode** (default): Spawns HTTP server, communicates via fetch()\n   - **Direct mode**: Single process, calls `SessionPrompt.prompt()` directly\n\n5. **Event Flow**\n   - `Bus.subscribeAll()` listens to session events: `message.part.updated`, `session.idle`, `session.error`\n   - Events transformed to JSON output: `step_start`, `text`, `tool_use`, `step_finish`, `error`\n   - Format controlled by `--json-standard` (opencode or claude)\n\n### 4. DEFAULT_TIMEOUT, MAX_TIMEOUT);\n   \n   const timeoutTimer = setTimeout(() => {\n     timedOut = true;\n     void killTree();  // Kill process group\n   }, timeout);\n   ```\n\n3. **Continuous mode polling** (`continuous-mode.js`):\n   ```javascript\n   const checkRunning = setInterval(() => {\n     if (!stdinReader.isRunning()) {\n       // Wait for pending messages to complete\n       const waitForPending = () => {\n         if (!isProcessing && pendingMessages.length === 0) {\n           resolve();\n         } else {\n           setTimeout(waitForPending, 100);  // Polls every 100ms\n         }\n       };\n       waitForPending();\n     }\n   }, 100);\n   ```\n\n4. **Input queue merge delay** (`input-queue.js`):\n   ```javascript\n   this.mergeDelayMs = options.mergeDelayMs || 50;  // Wait 50ms for more lines\n   this.mergeTimer = setTimeout(() => {\n     this.flushPendingLines();\n   }, this.mergeDelayMs);\n   ```\n\n**Issue #146 Context:**\n- Process hung indefinitely after completing work\n- System message shows \"✅ Agent command completed\" at 15:37 but process didn't exit until manually killed ~2 hours later\n- Root cause: Some waitable resource (session.idle event?) not firing or not being properly awaited\n\n### 5. 376→  systemMessage,\n   377→  appendSystemMessage,\n   378→  jsonStandard\n   379→) {\n   380→  const compactJson = argv['compact-json'] === true;\n   381→\n   382→  // Start server like OpenCode    throw new Error('Failed to create session');\n   410→      }\n   411→    }\n   412→\n   413→    // Create event handler for the selected JSON standard\n   414→    const eventHandler = 418→      createBusEventSubscription({\n   419→        sessionID,\n   420→        eventHandler,\n   421→        onError: () => {\n   422→          hasError = true;\n   423→        },\n   424→ 456→\n   457→    // Wait for session to become idle\n   458→    await eventPromise;\n   459→  } finally {\n   460→    // Always clean up resources\n   461→    if (unsub) {\n   462→      unsub();\n   463→    }\n   464→    server.stop();\n   465→    await Instance.dispose();\n   466→  }\n   467→}\n   468→\n   469→async function runDirectMode(\n   470→  argv,\n   471→  request,\n   472→       "content": "/**\n * Continuous stdin mode for the Agent CLI.\n * Keeps the session alive and processes messages as they arrive.\n */\n\nimport { Server } from '../server/server.ts';\nimport { Instance } from '../project/instance.ts';\nimport { Bus } from '../bus/index.ts';\nimport { Session } from '../session/index.ts';\nimport { SessionPrompt } from '../session/prompt.ts';\nimport { createEventHandler } from '../json-standard/index.ts';\nimport { createContinuousStdinReader } from './input-queue.js';\nimport { Log } from '../util/log.ts';\nimport { Flag } from '../flag/flag.ts';\nimport { outputStatus, outputError, outputInput } from './output.ts';\n\n// Shared error tracking\nlet hasError = false;\n\n/**\n * Set error state\n * @param {boolean} value - Error state value\n */\nexport function setHasError(value) {\n  hasError = value;\n}\n\n/**\n * Get error state\n * @returns {boolean}\n */\nexport function getHasError() {\n  return hasError;\n}\n\n// outputStatus is now imported from './output.ts'\n// It outputs to stdout for non-error messages, stderr for errors\n\n// Logger for resume operations\nconst log = Log.create({ service: 'resume' });\n\n/**\n * Resolve the session to use based on --resume, --continue, and --no-fork options.\n * Returns the session ID to use, handling forking as needed.\n * @param {object} argv - Command line arguments\n * @param {boolean} compactJson - Whether to use compact JSON output\n * @returns {Promise<{sessionID: string, wasResumed: boolean, wasForked: boolean} | null>} - Session info or null if new session should be created\n * @export\n */\nexport async function resolveResumeSession(argv, compactJson) {\n  const resumeSessionID = argv.resume;\n  const shouldContinue = argv.continue === true;\n  const noFork = argv['no-fork'] === true;\n\n  // If neither --resume nor --continue is specified, return null to create new session\n  if (!resumeSessionID && !shouldContinue) {\n    return null;\n  }\n\n  let targetSessionID = resumeSessionID;\n\n  // If --continue is specified, find the most recent session\n  if (shouldContinue && !targetSessionID) {\n    let mostRecentSession = null;\n    let mostRecentTime = 0;\n\n    for await (const session of Session.list()) {\n      // Skip child sessions (those with parentID) - find top-level sessions only\n      if (session.parentID) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      if (session.time.updated > mostRecentTime) {\n        mostRecentTime = session.time.updated;\n        mostRecentSession = session;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (!mostRecentSession) {\n      outputError(\n        {\n          errorType: 'SessionNotFound',\n          message:\n            'No existing sessions found to continue. Start a new session first.',\n        },\n        compactJson\n      );\n      process.exit(1);\n    }\n\n    targetSessionID = mostRecentSession.id;\n    log.info(() => ({\n      message: 'Found most recent session to continue',\n      sessionID: targetSessionID,\n      title: mostRecentSession.title,\n    }));\n  }\n\n  // Verify the session exists\n  let existingSession;\n  try {\n    existingSession = await Session.get(targetSessionID);\n  } catch (_error) {\n    // Session.get throws an error when the session doesn't exist\n    outputError(\n      {\n        errorType: 'SessionNotFound',\n        message: `Session not found: ${targetSessionID}`,\n      },\n      compactJson\n    );\n    process.exit(1);\n  }\n\n  if (!existingSession) {\n    outputError(\n      {\n        errorType: 'SessionNotFound',\n        message: `Session not found: ${targetSessionID}`,\n      },\n      compactJson\n    );\n    process.exit(1);\n  }\n\n  log.info(() => ({\n    message: 'Resuming session',\n    sessionID: targetSessionID,\n    title: existingSession.title,\n    noFork,\n  }));\n\n  // If --no-fork is specified, continue in the same session\n  if (noFork) {\n    outputStatus(\n      {\n        type: 'status',\n        mode: 'resume',\n        message: `Continuing session without forking: ${targetSessionID}`,\n        sessionID: targetSessionID,\n        title: existingSession.title,\n        forked: false,\n      },\n      compactJson\n    );\n\n    return {\n      sessionID: targetSessionID,\n      wasResumed: true,\n      wasForked: false,\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Fork the session to a new UUID (default behavior)\n  const forkedSession = await Session.fork({\n    sessionID: targetSessionID,\n  });\n\n  outputStatus(\n    {\n      type: 'status',\n      mode: 'resume',\n      message: `Forked session ${targetSessionID} to new session: ${forkedSession.id}`,\n      originalSessionID: targetSessionID,\n      sessionID: forkedSession.id,\n      title: forkedSession.title,\n      forked: true,\n    },\n    compactJson\n  );\n\n  log.info(() => ({\n    message: 'Forked session',\n    originalSessionID: targetSessionID,\n    newSessionID: forkedSession.id,\n  }));\n\n  return {\n    sessionID: forkedSession.id,\n    wasResumed: true,\n    wasForked: true,\n  };\n}\n\n/**\n * Run server mode with continuous stdin input\n * Keeps the session alive and processes messages as they arrive\n */\nexport async function runContinuousServerMode(\n  argv,\n  providerID,\n  modelID,\n  systemMessage,\n  appendSystemMessage,\n  jsonStandard\n) {\n  // Check both CLI flag and environment variable for compact JSON mode\n  const compactJson = argv['compact-json'] === true || Flag.COMPACT_JSON();\n  const compactJson);\n\n    let sessionID;\n\n    if (resumeInfo) {\n      // Use the resumed/forked session\n      sessionID = resumeInfo.sessionID;\n    } else {\n      // Create a new session\n      const checkIdle();\n            resolve();\n          }\n        });\n      });\n\n      // Send message\n      fetch(\n        `http://${server.hostname}:${server.port}/session/${sessionID}/message`,\n         "content": "     1→/**\n     2→ * Input queue for managing continuous stdin input.\n     3→ * Supports queuing of multiple messages and auto-merging of rapidly arriving lines.\n     4→ */\n     5→export class InputQueue {\n     6→  constructor(options = {}) {\n     7→    this.queue = [];\n     8→    this.autoMerge = options.autoMerge !== false; // enabled by default\n     9→    this.mergeDelayMs = options.mergeDelayMs || 50; // delay to wait for more lines\n    10→    this.pendingLines = [];\n    11→    this.mergeTimer = null;\n    12→    this.onMessage = options.onMessage || (() => {});\n    13→    this.interactive = options.interactive !== false; // enabled by default\n    14→  }\n    15→\n    16→  /**\n    17→   * Parse input and determine if it's JSON or plain text\n    18→   * @param {string} input -       "content": "/**\n * Input queue for managing continuous stdin input.\n * Supports queuing of multiple messages and auto-merging of rapidly arriving lines.\n */\nexport class InputQueue {\n  constructor(options = {}) {\n    this.queue = [];\n    this.autoMerge = options.autoMerge !== false; // enabled by default\n    this.mergeDelayMs = options.mergeDelayMs || 50; // delay to wait for more lines\n    this.pendingLines = [];\n    this.mergeTimer = null;\n    this.onMessage = options.onMessage || (() => {});\n    this.interactive = options.interactive !== false; // enabled by default\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Parse input and determine if it's JSON or plain text\n   * @param {string} input - Raw input string\n   * @returns {object} - Parsed message object\n   */\n  parseInput(input) {\n    const trimmed = input.trim();\n    if (!trimmed) {\n      return null;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const parsed = JSON.parse(trimmed);\n      // If it has a message field, use it directly\n      if (typeof parsed === 'object' && parsed !== null) {\n        return parsed;\n      }\n      // Otherwise wrap it\n      return { message: JSON.stringify(parsed) };\n    } catch (_e) {\n      // Not JSON, treat as plain text message\n      return { message: trimmed };\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Add a line to the queue, potentially merging with pending lines\n   * @param {string} line - Input line\n   */\n  addLine(line) {\n    if (!this.interactive && !line.trim().startsWith('{')) {\n      // In non-interactive mode, only accept JSON\n      return;\n    }\n\n    if (this.autoMerge) {\n      // Add to pending lines and schedule merge\n      this.pendingLines.push(line);\n      this.scheduleMerge();\n    } else {\n      // No merging, queue immediately\n      const parsed = this.parseInput(line);\n      if (parsed) {\n        this.queue.push(parsed);\n        this.notifyMessage(parsed);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Schedule a merge of pending lines after a short delay\n   */\n  scheduleMerge() {\n    if (this.mergeTimer) {\n      clearTimeout(this.mergeTimer);\n    }\n    this.mergeTimer = setTimeout(() => {\n      this.flushPendingLines();\n    }, this.mergeDelayMs);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Flush pending lines into a single merged message\n   */\n  flushPendingLines() {\n    if (this.pendingLines.length === 0) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const mergedText = this.pendingLines.join('\\n');\n    this.pendingLines = [];\n    this.mergeTimer = null;\n\n    const parsed = this.parseInput(mergedText);\n    if (parsed) {\n      this.queue.push(parsed);\n      this.notifyMessage(parsed);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Immediately flush any pending lines (for shutdown)\n   */\n  flush() {\n    if (this.mergeTimer) {\n      clearTimeout(this.mergeTimer);\n      this.mergeTimer = null;\n    }\n    this.flushPendingLines();\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get next message from the queue\n   * @returns {object|null} - The message object\n   */\n  notifyMessage(message) {\n    if (this.onMessage) {\n      this.onMessage(message);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get queue size\n   * @returns {number}\n   */\n  size() {\n    return this.queue.length;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Create a continuous stdin reader that queues input lines\n * @param {object} options - Options for the reader\n * @returns {object} - Reader with queue and control methods\n */\n// Note: This function is prepared for future continuous input mode\nexport function createContinuousStdinReader(options = {}) {\n  const inputQueue = new InputQueue(options);\n  let isRunning = true;\n  let lineBuffer = '';\n\n  const handleData = (chunk) => {\n    if (!isRunning) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    lineBuffer += chunk.toString();\n    const lines = lineBuffer.split('\\n');\n\n    // Keep the last incomplete line in buffer\n    lineBuffer = lines.pop() || '';\n\n    // Process complete lines\n    for (const line of lines) {\n      if (line.trim()) {\n        inputQueue.addLine(line);\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleEnd = () => {\n    // Process any remaining data in buffer\n    if (lineBuffer.trim()) {\n      inputQueue.addLine(lineBuffer);\n    }\n    inputQueue.flush();\n    isRunning = false;\n  };\n\n  process.stdin.on('data', handleData);\n  process.stdin.on('end', handleEnd);\n  process.stdin.on('error', () => {\n    isRunning = false;\n  });\n\n  return {\n    queue: inputQueue,\n    stop: () => {\n      isRunning = false;\n      inputQueue.flush();\n      process.stdin.removeListener('data', handleData);\n      process.stdin.removeListener('end', handleEnd);\n    },\n    isRunning: () => isRunning,\n  };\n}\n",
